 	public void createDeepLink(ExternalLinkConfiguration linkConfiguration) {
 		try {
 			StringBuilder linkBuilder = new StringBuilder();
 			linkBuilder.append(linkConfiguration.getRetrieveMotorQuoteExternalUrl());
 			linkBuilder.append("?");
 			linkBuilder.append(linkConfiguration.getQuoteReferenceParameter());
 			linkBuilder.append("=");
 			linkBuilder.append(getDeeplinkQuoteRef());
 			linkBuilder.append("&");
 			linkBuilder.append(linkConfiguration.getPostCodeParameter());
 			linkBuilder.append("=");
 			linkBuilder.append(URLEncoder.encode(getDeeplinkPostcode(), "UTF-8"));
 			linkBuilder.append("&");
 			linkBuilder.append(linkConfiguration.getChecksumParameter());
 			linkBuilder.append("=");
 			linkBuilder.append(URLEncoder.encode(getDeeplinkChecksum(), "UTF-8"));
 			this.deeplink = linkBuilder.toString();
 		} catch (UnsupportedEncodingException e) {
 			RSALoggerFactory.getLogger(this.getClass()).log(NWAEventCode.TechnicalLogging.TECHNICAL_EXCEPTION, e);
 
 			throw new TechnicalException(NWAEventCode.TechnicalLogging.TECHNICAL_EXCEPTION, e);
 		}
 	}

 public class QuoteBuyAction extends MultiAction {

 	 * Reference data code for "No Licence Ever Held" option

 	/**
 	 * Name of the cookie used for quote persistence. Defaults to 'Q', but we
 	 * can use Spring DI to set to any name.
 	 * <p>
 	 * Using Spring DI makes it safer, storing it in the WebFlow scope objects
 	 * proved it sometimes was null.
 	 */
 	private String quotePersistenceCookieName = "Q";
 	
 	private static final String MONTH = "MONTH";
 
 	public String getQuotePersistenceCookieName() {
 		return quotePersistenceCookieName;
 	}
 
 	public void setQuotePersistenceCookieName(String name) {
 		quotePersistenceCookieName = name;
 	}
 
 	/**
 	 * Checks whether there's an 'active' quote in the user's session context.
 	 * <p>
 	 * This is implemented using the {@link #quotePersistenceCookieName quote
 	 * persistence cookie}. The method treats an expired or missing cookie as if
 	 * it were set to 'false'.
 	 * <p>
 	 * The result, a boolean is stored in the flow scope under
 	 * 'hasSummaryCookieStatus'.
 	 * 
 	 * @param requestContext
 	 * @return Always success
 	 */
 	public Event checkQuoteSummaryCookieStatus(RequestContext requestContext) {
 		final String cookieName = getQuotePersistenceCookieName();
 		final String cookieValue = MapConstant.TRUE_STRING;
 		boolean hasQuote = false; // the result
 		final Object request = requestContext.getExternalContext()
 				.getNativeRequest();
 		
 		// We always need here a new quote when going to quote summary
 		String newQuoteRequest = MapConstant.TRUE_STRING; 
 				//requestContext.getExternalContext()
 				//.getRequestParameterMap().get(NEW_QUOTE_PARAM);
 
 		final QuoteDecorator quote = (QuoteDecorator) requestContext
 				.getExternalContext().getSessionMap().get(MapConstant.SessionObjectConstants.SESSION_OBJECT_QUOTE);
 
 		if (MapConstant.TRUE_STRING.equals(newQuoteRequest)) {
 			// discard the existing quote!
 			requestContext.getFlowScope().put("quoteSummaryCookieStatus",
 					hasQuote);
 
 			requestContext.getExternalContext().getSessionMap().remove(MapConstant.SessionObjectConstants.SESSION_OBJECT_QUOTE);
 
 			disableCookie(requestContext);
 
 			return success();
 		} else {
 			if ((request instanceof HttpServletRequest) && (quote != null)) {
 				final HttpServletRequest httpRequest = (HttpServletRequest) request;
 
 				if (httpRequest.getCookies() != null) {
 					for (Cookie quoteAndBuyCookie : httpRequest.getCookies()) {
 						if (cookieName.equals(quoteAndBuyCookie.getName())
 								&& (cookieValue.equals(quoteAndBuyCookie
 										.getValue()))) {
 							requestContext.getFlowScope().put(MapConstant.SessionObjectConstants.SESSION_OBJECT_QUOTE, quote);
 							hasQuote = true;
 							break;
 						}
 					}
 				}
 			}
 
 			requestContext.getFlowScope().put("quoteSummaryCookieStatus",
 					hasQuote);
 
 			return success();
 		}
 	}
 
 	/**
 	 * Sets the persistence cookie's value to 'true'. This value is checked
 	 * through Spring WebFlow in the 'checkCookie' decision state.
 	 * <p>
 	 * Also updates the web session to store the quote object.
 	 * 
 	 * @param requestContext
 	 *            Provided by Spring WebFlow
 	 * @return Always success
 	 */
 	public Event enableCookie(RequestContext requestContext) {
 		final String cookieName = getQuotePersistenceCookieName();
 		final Object response = requestContext.getExternalContext()
 				.getNativeResponse();
 
 		if (response instanceof HttpServletResponse) {
 			final Cookie c = new Cookie(cookieName, MapConstant.TRUE_STRING);
 
 			c.setPath("/");
 			((HttpServletResponse) response).addCookie(c);
 		}
 
 		final QuoteDecorator quote = (QuoteDecorator) requestContext
 				.getFlowScope().get(MapConstant.SessionObjectConstants.SESSION_OBJECT_QUOTE);
 		requestContext.getExternalContext().getSessionMap().put(MapConstant.SessionObjectConstants.SESSION_OBJECT_QUOTE, quote);
 
 		return success();
 	}
 
 	/**
 	 * Sets the persistence cookie's value to 'false'.
 	 * <p>
 	 * Also clears the quote object from the web session.
 	 * 
 	 * @param requestContext
 	 * @return Always success
 	 */
 	public Event disableCookie(RequestContext requestContext) {
 		final String cookieName = getQuotePersistenceCookieName();
 		final Object response = requestContext.getExternalContext()
 				.getNativeResponse();
 		final Object request = requestContext.getExternalContext()
 				.getNativeRequest();
 
 		if (response instanceof HttpServletResponse) {
 
 			// value doesn't matter, as we remove the cookie
 			final Cookie c = new Cookie(cookieName, "false");
 
 			c.setPath("/");
 			c.setMaxAge(0);
 			((HttpServletResponse) response).addCookie(c);
 		}
 
 		// set to false quote cookie in current request
 		if (request instanceof HttpServletRequest) {
 			Cookie[] cookies = ((HttpServletRequest) request).getCookies();
 			if (cookies != null) {
 				for (Cookie cookie : cookies) {
 					if (cookieName.equals(cookie.getName())) {
 						cookie.setValue("false");
 					}
 				}
 			}
 		}
 
 		requestContext.getExternalContext().getSessionMap().remove(MapConstant.SessionObjectConstants.SESSION_OBJECT_QUOTE);
 		return success();
 	}

 		return new Event(this, "marsEligible");
 	}
 
 	public void reRate(Quote quote, RequestContext requestContext){
 
 		quote.setTriggerCorrespondenceService(false);
 
 	}
 
 
 	public boolean validateRequest(String quoteNumber, String postCode,
 			String checksum, String key) {
 		boolean result = false;
 
 		if (checksum == null) {
 			return false;
 		}
 
 		if ((quoteNumber != null) && (postCode != null)) {
 			quoteNumber = quoteNumber.trim();
 			postCode = postCode.trim();
 
 			String checksumContent = quoteNumber + postCode;
 
 			String generatedChecksum = HashingService.getHMACSHA1(
 					checksumContent, key, HashingService.ISO_LATIN);
 
 			if (generatedChecksum.equals(checksum)) {
 				result = true;
 			}
 		}
 		return result;
 	}
 
 
 	public Event preCaptureDetails(RequestContext requestContext) {
 		Map<String, Map<String, DataItem>> refDataItem = getRefDataGroups("captureDetails");
 		Map<String, Map<String, String>> refData = refDataService
 				.getRefData(refDataItem);
 
 		requestContext.getRequestScope().put("refDataItem", refDataItem);
 		requestContext.getRequestScope().put("refData", refData);
 
 		
 		//TODO: Irina -why do we have left over error messages when coming from quote summary? 
 		requestContext.getMessageContext().clearMessages();
 		
 
 		return success();
 	}
 
 	/**
 	 * Calls MotorQuote.ApplyFor first time through, then subsequently
 	 * MotorQuote.Requote, based on whether or not quote.quoteNumber is
 	 * populated: if MotorQuote.ApplyFor is called then quoteNumber is returned,
 	 * subsequently we have this value to use for MotorQuote.Requote.
 	 * 
 	 * @param quote
 	 *            Quote form bean
 	 * @param motorQuoteService
 	 *            IMotorQuoteService - business service class
 	 */
 
 	public Event preQuoteSummary(RequestContext requestContext){
 		
 		QuoteDecorator quote = (QuoteDecorator) requestContext.getFlowScope()
 				.get(MapConstant.SessionObjectConstants.SESSION_OBJECT_QUOTE);
 		quoteSummaryService.getQuoteSummary(quote);
 		quote.preProcessQuote(refDataService);
 
 		// ALEX_SEEL_CRTAG
 		String agents=setDefaultFromReferenceData(quote.getAgentId(),
 				refDataService, defaultRefDataCategoryKey, channelDefaultsKey,
 				agentIdKey);
 		if (MapConstant.SaturnWedEventConstants.WEDDING.equals(petContext.getMode())) {
 			quote.setAgentId(agents.split(",")[0]);
 		} else {
 			quote.setAgentId(agents.split(",")[1]);
 		}
 
 		quote.setRouteOfSale(setDefaultFromReferenceData(
 				quote.getRouteOfSale(), refDataService,
 				defaultRefDataCategoryKey, channelDefaultsKey, routeOfSaleKey));
 
 		//TODO: Irina - optimise - don't loadgrouops each time
 		quote.setCoreCovers(setDefaultFromReferenceData(
 				quote.getCoreCovers(), refDataService,
 				"default", "COVERLEVELTOCOVER", "NWA_WAE"));
 		
 		if (TypeHelper.isEmpty(quote.getQuoteNumber())) {
 			quote.setTriggerCorrespondenceService(true);
 			quote.setTriggerCorrespondenceService(false);
 		} else {
 			if (!quote.getCustomerEligibleForMonthlyPayments()) {
 				quote.setShowAnnually(Boolean.TRUE);
 			}
 		}
 
 		refDataUtility.referenceDataConversionsPostProcessor(quote);
 		quote.setDefaultSelectedLevel();
 		quote.setRenewalDate();
 		
 		return success();
 	}
 
 	/**
 	 * Calls Party.Validate to see if the user is recognized as an existing
 	 * echoice user in order to make changes in UI like set Yes/No for existing
 	 * user and make readonly the email field
 	 * 
 	 * 
 	 * @param quote
 	 *            Quote form bean
 	 * @param partyValidateService
 	 *            partyValidateService - business service class
 	 */
 	public Event prePaymentSummary(RequestContext requestContext) {
 		
 		QuoteDecorator quote = (QuoteDecorator) requestContext.getFlowScope()
 				.get(MapConstant.SessionObjectConstants.SESSION_OBJECT_QUOTE);
 		partyValidateService.validateParty(quote);
 		if (quote.getPaymentDetails().getCardType() == null) {
 			quote.getPaymentDetails().setCardType(
 					MapConstant.PaymentControllerConstants.DC_CARD_TYPE);
 		}
 
 		return success();
 	}
 
 	/**
 	 * Gets defaults from reference data and returns the default value - but
 	 * only if the current value is empty
 	 * 
 	 * @param referenceDataService
 	 * @param category
 	 * @param key
 	 * @return
 	 * 
 	 **/
 	public String setDefaultFromReferenceData(String currentValue,
 			IReferenceDataService referenceDataService, String loadGroup,
 			String category, String key) {
 
 		String referenceDataValue = null;
 
 		if (TypeHelper.isEmpty(currentValue)) {
 			IApplicationWhiteLabelContext context = ContextHolder.getContext();
 
 			Map<String, Map<String, DataItem>> refDataItems = referenceDataService
 					.loadGroups(loadGroup, context.getBrand(),
 							context.getProduct());
 			Map<String, DataItem> refData = refDataItems.get(category);
 
 			if (refData != null) {
 				DataItem dataItem = refData.get(key);
 				referenceDataValue = dataItem.getDecode();
 			} else {
 				referenceDataValue = currentValue;
 			}
 		} else {
 			referenceDataValue = currentValue;
 		}
 
 		return referenceDataValue;
 	}
 
 	public Event renderCaptureDetails(RequestContext requestContext){
 		
 		QuoteDecorator quote = (QuoteDecorator) requestContext.getFlowScope()
 				.get(MapConstant.SessionObjectConstants.SESSION_OBJECT_QUOTE);
 		Map<String, Map<String, DataItem>> refDataItem = getRefDataGroups("captureDetails");
 		Map<String, Map<String, String>> refData = refDataService
 				.getRefData(refDataItem);
 		requestContext.getRequestScope().put("refDataItem", refDataItem);
 		requestContext.getRequestScope().put("refData", refData);
 
 		refDataUtility.filterYears(refData, "YEAR", "DetailsCaptureDOB_Years",
 				NumberConstants.NEGATIVE_EIGHTY, NumberConstants.NEGATIVE_EIGHTEEN, CalendarConstants.DEFAULT_YEAR_OPTION);
 		refDataUtility.addDefaultToMonths(refData, MONTH,
 				"DetailsCaptureDOB_Months", "MM");
 		refDataUtility.addDefaultToDays(refData, "DAY",
 				"DetailsCaptureDOB_Days", "DD");
 		refDataUtility.filterYears(refData, "YEAR", "CoverStartDate_Years", NumberConstants.NEGATIVE_TWO,
 				1, CalendarConstants.DEFAULT_YEAR_OPTION);
 		refDataUtility.addDefaultToMonths(refData, MONTH,
 				"CoverStartDate_Months", "MM");
 		refDataUtility.addDefaultToDays(refData, "DAY", "CoverStartDate_Days",
 				"DD");
 		
 		// add MM for residency since
 		refDataUtility.addDefaultToMonths(refData, MONTH, MONTH, "MM");
 
 		refDataUtility.applyRestrictions(quote, refData);
 		
 		clearPolicyHolderData(quote);
 
 		return success();
 	}

 	}

 		if (!TypeHelper.isTrue(quote.getCustomized())) {

 		}
 
 		quote.calculateTotalPremium(selectedBundle);
 
 		return success();
 	}

 	/**
 	 * Update time of quote.policy.coverStartDate
 	 * 
 	 * @param quote
 	 *            Quote to update
 	 */
 	public Event updatePolicyCoverStartTime(RequestContext requestContext) {
 		QuoteDecorator quote = (QuoteDecorator) requestContext.getFlowScope()
 				.get(MapConstant.SessionObjectConstants.SESSION_OBJECT_QUOTE);
 
 		FormDate coverStartDate = quote.getPolicy().getCoverStartDate();
 		if (!isDateInFuture(coverStartDate.getCalendar())) {
 			// coverStartDate is today: set time of quote.policy.coverStartDate
 			// to that sent to netbanx
 			FormDate paymentTimeStamp = quote.getPolicy().getPaymentTimestamp();
 			coverStartDate.setHour(paymentTimeStamp.getHour());
 			coverStartDate.setMinute(paymentTimeStamp.getMinute());
 			coverStartDate.setSecond(paymentTimeStamp.getSecond());
 			coverStartDate.setMillisecond(paymentTimeStamp.getMillisecond());
 		} else {
 			// coverStartDate is in future: set time of
 			// quote.policy.coverStartDate to 00.01
 			coverStartDate.setHour(0);
 			coverStartDate.setMinute(1);
 			coverStartDate.setSecond(0);
 			coverStartDate.setMillisecond(0);
 		}
 
 		return success();
 	}
 
 
 	/**
 	 * Returns true if the provided calendar is in the future
 	 * 
 	 * @param cal
 	 *            Calendar
 	 * @return True if cal is in the future
 	 */
 	private boolean isDateInFuture(Calendar cal) {
 		boolean isDateInFuture = false;
 		if (cal != null) {
 			Calendar tomorrow = Calendar.getInstance();
 			tomorrow.set(Calendar.HOUR_OF_DAY, 0);
 			tomorrow.set(Calendar.MINUTE, 0);
 			tomorrow.set(Calendar.SECOND, 0);
 			tomorrow.set(Calendar.MILLISECOND, 0);
 			tomorrow.add(Calendar.DAY_OF_YEAR, 1);
 
 			isDateInFuture = cal.getTimeInMillis() >= tomorrow
 					.getTimeInMillis();
 		}
 		return isDateInFuture;
 	}
 
 	private Map<String, Map<String, DataItem>> getRefDataGroups(
 			String functionalArea) {
 		Map<String, Map<String, DataItem>> groups = refDataService.loadGroups(
 				functionalArea, ContextHolder.getContext().getBrand(),
 				ContextHolder.getContext().getProduct());
 		return groups;
 	}

 	/**
 	 * Fix for bug 291 ( & 704) Please place here any "alteration" code e.g. to
 	 * be executed after pressing "Get a quote" button in order to set default
 	 * values
 	 * 
 	 * @param quote
 	 *            - quote decorator
 	 */
 
 	public Event setupValuesFromString(RequestContext requestContext){
 		
 		QuoteDecorator quote = (QuoteDecorator) requestContext.getFlowScope()
 				.get(MapConstant.SessionObjectConstants.SESSION_OBJECT_QUOTE);
 		
 		Party policyHolder;
 		
 		if (quote.getGenericEvent() != null && quote.getGenericEvent() instanceof Wedding) {
 			Wedding wedding = (Wedding)quote.getGenericEvent();
 			if (wedding.getAreYouGettingMarried()) {
 				policyHolder = wedding.getParticipant1();
 			}
 			else{
 				policyHolder = quote.getPolicyHolder();
 			}
 		}
 		else{
 			policyHolder = quote.getPolicyHolder();
 		}
 
 		// if title is Mr, default gender to Male; similar for Ms or Miss or Mrs
 		// Note: we need to do this for the policy holder AND the additional
 		// drivers, if any
 		defaultGenderBasedOnTitle(policyHolder);
 
 		setUpperAndRemoveAllSpacePromoCodeJsOff(quote);
 		
 		validateHideValueForPromoCodeBasedOnAffiliate(quote);
 		
 		return success();
 	}
 
 
 	public void resetFirstAccessFromAgg(RequestContext requestContext) {
 		Boolean showAggIcon = (Boolean) requestContext.getFlowScope().get(
 				"showAggIcon");
 		if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(showAggIcon)) {
 			requestContext.getFlowScope().put("showAggIcon", Boolean.FALSE);
 		}
 	}
 
 	public static void defaultGenderBasedOnTitle(Party who) {
 		if (!TypeHelper.isEmpty(who.getTitle())) {
 			
 
 				if(MapConstant.SaturnWedEventConstants.WE_GENDER_REQUIRING_TITLE_CODES.indexOf("" + who.getTitle() + ",") < 0){
 				
 					boolean genderFemaleCheck = MapConstant.SaturnWedEventConstants.GENDER_FEMALE_TITLE_MARRIED.equals(who.getTitle())
 							|| MapConstant.SaturnWedEventConstants.GENDER_FEMALE_TITLE_SINGLE.equals(who.getTitle())
 							|| MapConstant.SaturnWedEventConstants.GENDER_FEMALE_TITLE_MS.equals(who.getTitle());
 					
 				if (MapConstant.SaturnWedEventConstants.GENDER_MALE_TITLE.equals(who.getTitle())
 					|| MapConstant.SaturnWedEventConstants.GENDER_MALE_FATHER.equals(who.getTitle())
 					|| MapConstant.SaturnWedEventConstants.GENDER_MALE_LORD.equals(who.getTitle())
 					|| MapConstant.SaturnWedEventConstants.GENDER_MALE_SIR.equals(who.getTitle())) {
 						
 					who.setGender(MapConstant.SaturnWedEventConstants.GENDER_MALE);
 						
 				} else if (genderFemaleCheck || MapConstant.SaturnWedEventConstants.GENDER_FEMALE_TITLE_DAME.equals(who.getTitle())
 					|| MapConstant.SaturnWedEventConstants.GENDER_FEMALE_TITLE_LADY.equals(who.getTitle())) {
 						
 					who.setGender(MapConstant.SaturnWedEventConstants.GENDER_FEMALE);
 				}
 			}
 		}
 	}

 	/**
 	 * Method called when requesting a quote. Triggered by click on
 	 * "Get Your Quote" in detailsCapture page.
 	 * 
 	 * @param quote 
 	 * 			  Contains the quote used for the Quote Search BS call
 	 */
 	public void getYourQuoteService(Quote quote) {
 		if (quote.getQuoteNumber() == null) {
 			applyForWAEQuoteTaskApplyForTaskService.applyForWAEQuoteTaskApplyForTask(quote);
 		} else {
 			requoteWAEQuoteTaskRequoteTaskService.requoteWAEQuoteTaskRequoteTask(quote);
 		}
 	}
 	
 	/**
 	 * After retrieve one of monthly / annual prices may be 0 as AIS doesn't
 	 * send it for quote retrieval. In such a case we do a requote, just to get
 	 * the updated prices for both frequencies.
 	 * 
 	 * @param quote
 	 * @return True if a price re-calculation is needed after retrieval
 	 */
 	public final boolean requiresPriceUpdatesAfterRetrieve(final Quote quote) {
 		
 		boolean customerEligibleForMonthlyPayments = Boolean.TRUE.equals(quote
 				.getCustomerEligibleForMonthlyPayments())
 				&& Boolean.TRUE.equals(quote.getShowAnnually()) && (quote
 				.getPolicy().getBaseMonthlyPremium() == null || quote
 				.getPolicy().getBaseMonthlyPremium() == 0.0D);
 		
 		boolean quoteNotAnnually = Boolean.FALSE.equals(quote.getShowAnnually()) && (quote
 				.getPolicy().getBaseAnnualPremium() == null || quote
 				.getPolicy().getBaseAnnualPremium() == 0.0D);
 		
 		return customerEligibleForMonthlyPayments || quoteNotAnnually;
 	}

 	 *            the quote
 	 */
 	public void blockAndUpdateQuoteStatus(QuoteDecorator quote) {
 		quote.setPaymentDone(false);
 		quote.setBlock(true);

 		updateQuoteStatusService.updateStatusUpdateQuoteStatus(quote);
 	}

 	/**
 	 * Unblock current quote, Quote block/unblock CR.
 	 * 
 	 * @param quote
 	 *            the quote
 	 */
 	public void unblockAndUpdateQuoteStatus(QuoteDecorator quote) {
 		if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(quote.getBlock())) {
 			quote.setPaymentDone(false);
 			quote.setBlock(false);
 			quote.setQuotePriority(1);
 			updateQuoteStatusService.updateStatusUpdateQuoteStatus(quote);
 		}
 	}

 	/**
 	 * Loads quoteMovementUpdateDate from conversation scope. PGLS defect 153,
 	 * Block/Unblock: Quote blocked incorrectly at Payment Screen
 	 * 
 	 * @param requestContext
 	 */
 	private void loadQuoteMovementUpdateDateFromConversation(
 			Quote quote, MutableAttributeMap conversationScope) {
 		FormDate quoteMovementUpdateDate = (FormDate) conversationScope
 				.get(MapConstant.ControllerConstants.QUOTE_MOVEMENT_UPDATE_DATE);
 		if ((quoteMovementUpdateDate != null)
 				&& (quote.getQuoteMovementUpdateDate() != null)
 				&& (quoteMovementUpdateDate.getTransformDate().compare(
 						quote.getQuoteMovementUpdateDate().getTransformDate()) > 0)) {
 			quote.setQuoteMovementUpdateDate(quoteMovementUpdateDate);
 		}
 	}
 
 	/**
 	 * Saves quoteMovementUpdateDate to conversation scope. PGLS defect 153,
 	 * Block/Unblock: Quote blocked incorrectly at Payment Screen
 	 * 
 	 * @param requestContext
 	 */
 	private void saveQuoteMovementUpdateDateToConversation(
 			Quote quote, MutableAttributeMap conversationScope) {
 		conversationScope.put(
 				MapConstant.ControllerConstants.QUOTE_MOVEMENT_UPDATE_DATE,
 				quote.getQuoteMovementUpdateDate());
 	}
 
 	public Event schedulePayment(RequestContext requestContext){
 		QuoteDecorator quote = (QuoteDecorator) requestContext.getFlowScope()
 		.get(MapConstant.SessionObjectConstants.SESSION_OBJECT_QUOTE);
 		MutableAttributeMap conversationScope=requestContext.getConversationScope();
 		
 		loadQuoteMovementUpdateDateFromConversation(quote, conversationScope);
 		paymentScheduleService.schedulePayment(quote);
 		saveQuoteMovementUpdateDateToConversation(quote, conversationScope);
 		
 		return success();
 	}

 	/**
 	 * Populate policyHolder data in case when 'AreYouGettingMarried' == true</br>
 	 * @param quote
 	 */
 	public void fillPolicyHolderData(QuoteDecorator quote) {
 		
 		if (quote == null) {
 			return;
 		}
 		
 		if (quote.getGenericEvent() != null && quote.getGenericEvent() instanceof Wedding) {
 			
 			Wedding wedding = (Wedding)quote.getGenericEvent();
 			Party policyHolder = quote.getPolicyHolder();
 			
 			if (wedding.getAreYouGettingMarried()) {
 				
 				policyHolder.setFirstname(wedding.getParticipant1().getFirstname());
 				policyHolder.setSurname(wedding.getParticipant1().getSurname());
 				policyHolder.setTitle(wedding.getParticipant1().getTitle());
 				FormDate dateOfBirth=new FormDate();
 				dateOfBirth.setCalendar(wedding.getParticipant1().getDateOfBirth().getCalendar());
 				policyHolder.setDateOfBirth(dateOfBirth);
 				policyHolder.setGender(wedding.getParticipant1().getGender());
 			}
 		}
 	}
 
 	public void clearPolicyHolderData(Quote quote) {
 		if (quote != null 
 			&& quote.getGenericEvent() != null 
 			&& quote.getGenericEvent() instanceof Wedding) {
 			
 			Wedding wedding = (Wedding)quote.getGenericEvent();
 			Party policyHolder = quote.getPolicyHolder();
 			
 			if (wedding.getAreYouGettingMarried()) {
 				
 				policyHolder.setFirstname(null);
 				policyHolder.setSurname(null);
 				policyHolder.setTitle(null);
 				policyHolder.setDateOfBirth(new FormDate(true));
 				policyHolder.setGender(null);
 			}
 		}
 	}
 	
 	
 	
 	/**
 	 * Because - on JSOFF - we need to handle some scenarios (handled on UI
 	 * side when JSON) - we need to re-set the selected optional extras.
 	 * 
 	 * @param quote
 	 * @param requestContext
 	 * @throws Exception
 	 */
 	public void setCustomOptionalExtras(Quote quote, RequestContext requestContext){
 		
 		if (MapConstant.TRUE_STRING.equals(requestContext.getExternalContext().getRequestParameterMap().get("isJSOFF"))) {
 			String marqueeRequest = requestContext.getExternalContext().getRequestParameterMap().get("selectedOptionalCoverMarquee");
 			String overseasRequest = requestContext.getExternalContext().getRequestParameterMap().get("selectedOptionalCoverOverseas");
 			String subCoverRequest = requestContext.getExternalContext().getRequestParameterMap().get("selectedOptionalSubCover");
 			if (marqueeRequest != null && overseasRequest != null) {
 				
 				quote.setSelectedOptionalCoverMarqueeJSOFF(marqueeRequest);
 				quote.setSelectedOptionalCoverOverseasJSOFF(overseasRequest);
 				quote.setSelectedOptionalSubCover(subCoverRequest);
 			}
 			if (marqueeRequest != null && subCoverRequest == null) {
 				quote.setSelectedOptionalCoverMarqueeJSOFF(marqueeRequest);
 			
 			}
 			if (marqueeRequest == null && subCoverRequest != null) {
 				quote.setSelectedOptionalCoverMarqueeJSOFF(marqueeRequest);
 				quote.setSelectedOptionalSubCover(subCoverRequest);
 				if (overseasRequest != null) {
 					quote.setSelectedOptionalCoverOverseasJSOFF(overseasRequest);
 				}
 			}
 		}
 	}
 	
 	public boolean setRemoveAddButton(Quote quote){
 		boolean removeAdd = false;
 		
 		String marqueeRequest = quote.getSelectedOptionalCoverMarquee();
 		String overseasRequest = quote.getSelectedOptionalCoverOverseas();
 		
 		
-		if (marqueeRequest == null && overseasRequest == null) {			
+		if (marqueeRequest != null) {

 	private void setUpperAndRemoveAllSpacePromoCodeJsOff(Quote quote){
 		if (!StringUtils.isBlank(quote.getMarketingCode())){
 			//remove all spaces
 			quote.setMarketingCode(quote.getMarketingCode().replaceAll(" ", ""));
 			//if the promoCode is not upperCase make him
 			if (!quote.getMarketingCode().toUpperCase().equals(quote.getMarketingCode())){
 			
 				quote.setMarketingCode(quote.getMarketingCode().toUpperCase());
 			}
 		}
 	}
 	
 	private void validateHideValueForPromoCodeBasedOnAffiliate(Quote quote){
 		
 		IWcmContentRetriever wcmContentRetriever = getWCMContentRetriver();
 		if (wcmContentRetriever == null){
 			return;
 		}
 		
 		if (!StringUtils.isEmpty(quote.getReferrerID()) && !StringUtils.isEmpty(quote.getMarketingCode())){
 			String wcmSimpleStringDisplayPromoCode = wcmContentRetriever.getContent(
 					AssetType.SIMPLE_STRING, "displayPromoCodeForAffiliate"+quote.getReferrerID()+"_"+petContext.getMode());
 			//if the promoCode field is hidden
 			if ("false".equals(wcmSimpleStringDisplayPromoCode) && !isValidPromoCode(quote)){
 				//if promoCode is not in the list of valid PromoCode then set the value to empty
 					quote.setMarketingCode("");
 				
 			}
 		}
 	}
 	
 	/**
 	 * Search if value from 'Promotional Code' field is on the ValidPromoCode list
 	 * 
 	 */
 	private boolean isValidPromoCode(Quote quote){
 		boolean isValid = false;
 		
 		IWcmContentRetriever wcmContentRetriever = getWCMContentRetriver();
 		if (wcmContentRetriever == null) {
 			return isValid;
 		}
 		
 		String wcmSimpleStringListOfValidPromoCode = wcmContentRetriever.getContent(
 				AssetType.SIMPLE_STRING, "listOfValidPromoCode_"+petContext.getMode());
 		
 		Pattern pattern = Pattern.compile("(\\[)(.*?)(\\])");
         Matcher matcher = pattern.matcher(wcmSimpleStringListOfValidPromoCode);
         
         String ruleMatches = new String();
 
         while(matcher.find())
         {
         	ruleMatches = matcher.group(2);
         	break;
         }
         
         if (!StringUtils.isBlank(ruleMatches)){
         	
 	        List<String> dataForMatchRule = Arrays.asList(ruleMatches.split(","));
 	        
 	        for (String promoCodeValid : dataForMatchRule){
 	        	 if (promoCodeValid.equalsIgnoreCase(quote.getMarketingCode())){
 	 	        	isValid = true;
 	 	        	break;
 	        	 }
 	        }
         }
         
 		return isValid;
 	}
 	
 	private IWcmContentRetriever getWCMContentRetriver(){
 		ServletRequest servletRequest = ContextHolder.getServletRequest();
 		if (!(servletRequest instanceof HttpServletRequest)) {
 			// this point should never be reached
 			return null;
 		}
 		HttpSession session = ((HttpServletRequest) servletRequest).getSession();
 		ServletContext servletContext = session.getServletContext();
 		WebApplicationContext wac = WebApplicationContextUtils
 				.getRequiredWebApplicationContext(servletContext);
 		return (IWcmContentRetriever) wac.getBean("wcmContentRetriever");
 	}
 	
 	// the length of Brand from URL must be equals with 4 to used it
 	public String checkLengthForAffiliate(String affiliateName){
 		if (affiliateName != null && affiliateName.length() == MapConstant.ValidatorConstants.MAX_REFERRERID_LENGHT_URL_PARAM){
 			return affiliateName;
 		}
 		else {
 			return null;
 		}
 	}
 	
 	public void sendEmail(final QuoteDecorator quote) {
 		communicationSendCorrespondenceService.sendEmail(quote);
 	}

 function helpOn(elementId) {
 	var fieldWithHelp = $('#' + elementId).closest('.fieldWithHelp');
 	if (fieldWithHelp.hasClass('helpOn')) {
 		fieldWithHelp.removeClass('helpOn');
 	} else {
 		fieldWithHelp.addClass('helpOn');
 	}
 }
 
 function switchButtonEnable(button, enable) {
 	button.attr("disabled", enable ? "true" : "");
 	disabledClassOnWrapper(button, enable);
 }
 
 function disabledClassOnWrapper(button, disabled) {
 	var buttonWrapper = button.closest('.btn');
 	if (buttonWrapper.length) {
 		if (disabled) {
 			buttonWrapper.addClass("disabled");
 		} else {
 			buttonWrapper.removeClass("disabled");
 		}
 	}
 }
 
 function toggleOverlay(overlay, show) {
 	if (show) {
 		overlay.addClass("show");
 	} else {
 		overlay.removeClass("show");
 	}
 }
 
 var createGroupedArray = function(arr, chunkSize) {
     var groups = [], i;
     for (i = 0; i < arr.length; i += chunkSize) {
         groups.push(arr.slice(i, i + chunkSize));
     }
     return groups;
 }
 
 var coverDetailsPanelGroupIndex = function(arr, itemSelectedIndex) { 
  for (i = 0; i < arr.length; i ++) {
         if(arr[i].indexOf(itemSelectedIndex)>-1) {
          return i;
        }
     } 
 }
 
 var getMarkedPositionOnLoad = function(elem){
 	var selectedElementIndex=0;
 	var userItemsIndexes = []
 	
 	elem.children().each(function( index, element ) {
 		userItemsIndexes.push(index);		
     	if($(element).hasClass('selected')) {
     		selectedElementIndex = index;
     	}
 	});
 	
 	var groupedCarouselArr = createGroupedArray(userItemsIndexes, noItems);
 	var coverDetailsPanelIndex = coverDetailsPanelGroupIndex(groupedCarouselArr, selectedElementIndex);
 
 	return groupedCarouselArr[coverDetailsPanelIndex][0];
 }
 
 var executed = false;
 var markedPosition = 0;
 var noItems = 3;
 
 
 $(window).resize(function(){
     if ($(window).width() <= 414) {
     	noItems = 1;
     }
     else if(($(window).width() > 414) && ($(window).width() <= 768)) {
     	noItems = 2;
     } else {
     	noItems = 3;
     }
  
 });
 
 
 
 function startOwlCarousel() {
 	var owl = $("#coverLevelsDetails");
 	owl.owlCarousel({
 	    items : noItems,
 	    touchDrag  : false,
 	    mouseDrag  : false,
 	    afterInit : function(elem) {
 	    	if(!executed){		  
 	        	markedPosition = getMarkedPositionOnLoad(this.$owlItems);
 	    	}
 	    	this.owlControls.hide();
         	this.jumpTo(markedPosition);
 	    },
 	    afterAction: function(el){
             //remove class active
             this.$owlItems.removeClass('first');
             this.$owlItems.removeClass('last');  
             //add class first and last
 	        this.$owlItems.eq(this.currentItem).addClass('first');
 	        this.$owlItems.eq(this.currentItem + (this.owl.visibleItems.length - 1)).addClass('last');
       }
 	});
+
+	var totalElements = $('#coverLevelsDetails .owl-wrapper .owl-item').length;
+	var prevEl = $(".prevLevel");
+	var nextEl = $(".nextLevel");
+	var hiddenClass = "hidden-element";
+	var numberOfCoversVisible = 3;
+	if(totalElements <= numberOfCoversVisible){
+		if (!prevEl.hasClass(hiddenClass)) {
+			prevEl.addClass(hiddenClass);
+		}
+		if (!nextEl.hasClass(hiddenClass)) {
+			nextEl.addClass(hiddenClass);
+		}
+	}
+	var positionOfCarousel = 0;
+	if(positionOfCarousel === 0){
+		if (!prevEl.hasClass(hiddenClass)) {
+			prevEl.addClass(hiddenClass);
+		}
+	}
 	$(".nextLevel").click(function(){
 		executed = true;
 		owl.trigger('owl.next');
+		positionOfCarousel++;
+		if(positionOfCarousel > 0 && positionOfCarousel + numberOfCoversVisible <= totalElements){
+			if (prevEl.hasClass(hiddenClass)) {
+				prevEl.removeClass(hiddenClass);
+			}
+			if(positionOfCarousel + numberOfCoversVisible == totalElements){
+				if (!nextEl.hasClass(hiddenClass)) {
+					nextEl.addClass(hiddenClass);
+				}
+			}
+		}else{
+			positionOfCarousel = 0;
+			if (!prevEl.hasClass(hiddenClass)) {
+				prevEl.addClass(hiddenClass);
+			}
+		}
 	});
 	$(".prevLevel").click(function(){
 		executed = true;
 		owl.trigger('owl.prev');
+		positionOfCarousel--;
+		if(positionOfCarousel > 0){
+			if(positionOfCarousel + numberOfCoversVisible < totalElements){
+				if (prevEl.hasClass(hiddenClass)) {
+					prevEl.removeClass(hiddenClass);
+				}
+				if (nextEl.hasClass(hiddenClass)) {
+					nextEl.removeClass(hiddenClass);
+				}
+			}
+		}else{
+			positionOfCarousel = 0;
+			if (!prevEl.hasClass(hiddenClass)) {
+				prevEl.addClass(hiddenClass);
+			}
+		}
 	});
 }
 
 function stickHeaderOwlCarousel() {
 	var owl = $("#sticky-header-covers");
 	owl.owlCarousel({
 	    items : noItems,
 	    touchDrag  : false,
 	    mouseDrag  : false,
 	    afterInit : function(elem) {
 	    	if(!executed){		  
 	        	markedPosition = getMarkedPositionOnLoad(this.$owlItems);
 	    	}
 	    	this.owlControls.hide();
         	this.jumpTo(markedPosition);
         	
 	    },
 	    afterAction: function(el){
             //remove class active
             this.$owlItems.removeClass('first');
             this.$owlItems.removeClass('last');  
             //add class first and last
 	        this.$owlItems.eq(this.currentItem).addClass('first');
 	        this.$owlItems.eq(this.currentItem + (this.owl.visibleItems.length - 1)).addClass('last');
       }
 	});
 	$(".nextLevel").click(function(){
 		executed = true;
 		owl.trigger('owl.next');
 	});
 	$(".prevLevel").click(function(){
 		executed = true;
 		owl.trigger('owl.prev');
 	});
 	
 }
 
 
 
 // STICKY HEADER
 function toggleStikyHeader(){
 	
 if (!!$('#coverLevelsDetails').is(":visible")) { 
 	
 	var stickyTop = $('#coverLevelsDetails').offset().top + 150; 	
 	var stickyBottom = $('#coverLevelsDetails .optionalExtras').offset().top -40;
 	var stickyStop = !$('#exclusions .exclusionsSection').is(":visible")
 
 	$(window).scroll(function(){ 
 		var windowTop = $(window).scrollTop(); 
 		
 			if (windowTop > stickyTop && windowTop < stickyBottom && stickyStop){			
 				$('#sticky-header').addClass('fixed');
 				$('#coverLevelsDetails .coverLevelHeader.select-cover').css('visibility', 'hidden');
 				$('#coverLevelsDetailsSection .coverLevelsNavigation').css('visibility', 'hidden');				
 			} else {
 				$('#sticky-header').removeClass('fixed');
 				$('#coverLevelsDetails .coverLevelHeader.select-cover').css('visibility', 'visible');
 				$('#coverLevelsDetailsSection .coverLevelsNavigation').css('visibility', 'visible');
 			}	
 		
 	});
 }
 }
 
 
 function selectFirstRadio(element){
 	var elementId = element.attr('id');
 	$('input[id^="'+elementId+'_"]:first').attr('checked',true);
 }
 
 function selectOption(element){
 	element.attr('checked',true);
 	
 	$("input[type='checkbox']").not(element).attr('checked',false);
 	var el = $("input[type='checkbox']").not(element);
 
 	el.each(function(index,elem){
 		$('input[id^="'+elem.id+'"]').attr('checked',false);
 	});
 	PUB_SUB.trigger('sendExtrasDataOnClick',$(element));
 }
 
 function unselectOption(element){
 	var elementId = element.attr('id');
 	element.attr('checked',false);
 	element.attr('value',"");
 	$('input[id^="'+elementId+'"]').attr('checked',false);
 	PUB_SUB.trigger('sendExtrasDataOnClick',$(element));
 }
 
 function submitForm(element, eventId) {
 	var form = element.closest('form');
 	READY_TO_SUBMIT_FORM = false;
 
 	var fragments = "";
 	if ($(".JLW_QS.JLE_IDD").length) {
 		fragments = "preCoverLevelsEvent,coverLevelsEvent";
 	} else {
 		fragments = "preCoverLevels,coverLevels,exclusions";
 	}
 	
 	var objectsToHandle = [];
 	objectsToHandle[0] = function() { eventsForQuoteSummary(); };
 	objectsToHandle[1] = function() { READY_TO_SUBMIT_FORM=true;};
 	objectsToHandle[2] = function() { $("#optionalExtrasQS .helpMessageBox").hide(); };
 	objectsToHandle[3] = function() { 
 		$("#optionalExtrasQS input[type='checkbox'],#optionalExtrasQS input[type='radio']").click(function(){
 		$('html, body').animate({
 	        scrollTop: $("#coverLevels").offset().top
 	    }, 100);
 	}); };
 	
 	return ajaxSubmit(form.attr('id'),
 					  eventId,
 					  fragments,
 					  eventId, 
 					  "preventMultipleClick",
 					  null,
 					  null,
 					  null,
 					  objectsToHandle);
 	
 }
